
on_monthly_pulse_state = {
    on_actions = {
        assimilation_on_action
    }
}

assimilation_on_action = {
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = {
                is_incorporated = yes
                owner = {
                    any_primary_culture = {
                        has_discrimination_trait = anglophone
                    }
                    NOR = {
                        has_law = law_type:law_minority_rights_violent_hostility
                        has_law = law_type:law_minority_rights_ghettoization
                    }
                    NOT = {
                        any_primary_culture = {
                            has_discrimination_trait = african_heritage
                        }
                    }
                }
                any_scope_pop = {
                    culture = {
                        has_discrimination_trait = african_heritage
                        NOT = { has_homeland = ROOT }
                        NOT = { has_discrimination_trait = anglophone }
                    }
                    pop_acceptance >= 20
                    NOT = { has_ongoing_assimilation = yes }
                }
            }
            every_scope_pop = {
                limit = {
                    culture = {
                        has_discrimination_trait = african_heritage
                        NOT = { has_homeland = ROOT }
                        NOT = { has_discrimination_trait = anglophone }
                    }
                    pop_acceptance >= 20
                    NOT = { has_ongoing_assimilation = yes }
                }
                change_pop_culture = {
                    target = cu:anglo_african
                    value = pop_culture_conversion_propotion_script_value
                }
            }
        }

        if = {
            limit = {
                is_incorporated = yes
                owner = {
                    any_primary_culture = {
